As technology continues to advance at an unprecedented pace, it has led to more automation within various sectors, including healthcare. While this brings efficiency and precision, there is also the risk of diminishing the value of the artisanal craftsmanship that was once integral in many areas of medicine, such as surgical procedures or patient care where human touch plays a crucial role.
